style="height:1em;vertical-align:-0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">Q</span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathnormal">b</span><span class="mclose">)</span></span></span></span><span> true). Thus, </span><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>S</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">S</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.05764em;">S</span></span></span></span><span> is satisfiable, so the algorithm returns false, meaning </span><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi mathvariant="script">R</mi><mo>∪</mo><mi mathvariant="script">F</mi><mo>⊭</mo><mi>α</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathcal{R} \cup \mathcal{F} \not\models \alpha</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathcal">R</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">∪</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.8889em;vertical-align:-0.1944em;"></span><span class="mord mathcal" style="margin-right:0.09931em;">F</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel"><span class="mord vbox"><span class="thinbox"><span class="rlap"><span class="strut" style="height:0.8889em;vertical-align:-0.1944em;"></span><span class="inner"><span class="mord"><span class="mrel"></span></span></span><span class="fix"></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.999em;vertical-align:-0.249em;"></span><span class="mrel">⊨</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.4306em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.0037em;">α</span></span></span></span><span>.</span></p></li></ul><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>This algorithm systematically checks all possible models by leveraging the finite nature of the Herbrand universe. While it may be inefficient for large domains, it correctly solves the D-ENTAILMENT problem.</span></p>

### 用户

用中文讲解

---

### DeepSeek AI

<p>思考：</p><blockquote><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>我们被问到关于D-ENTAILMENT问题：给定一组析取规则R，一组事实F，和一个基原子α，我们想检查是否每个R∪F的模型都是α的模型。</span><br><span>注意：析取规则的形式为：∀x1...∀xk.(P1 ∧ ... ∧ Pn → Q1 ∨ ... ∨ Qm)，其中n,m&gt;=1，Pi和Qj是函数自由的原子，且Qj也可以是⊥（假）。</span><br><span>问题：每个R∪F的模型是否也是α的模型？即R∪F ⊧ α？</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>方法：我们可以通过检查R∪F ∪ {¬α}是否不可满足来解决这个问题。如果不可满足，则蕴含成立；否则不成立。</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>由于规则是函数自由的，我们可以将问题限制在赫尔布朗宇宙中，该宇宙由出现在F和R中的常量组成（如果没有常量，则引入一个虚拟常量）。</span><br><span>然后，我们可以将规则R相对于常量集进行基化，得到一组基规则G。那么问题归结为：G ∪ F ∪ {¬α}在命题逻辑中是否不可满足？</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>算法：</span></p><ol start="1"><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>令C为出现在F和R中的所有常量的集合。如果C为空，则引入一个虚拟常量c0。</span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>通过将每个规则中的变量用C中的常量替换，将R基化，得到一组基规则G。</span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>令S = G ∪ F ∪ {¬α}。</span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>检查S是否不可满足（即没有模型满足S）。如果是，则返回“是”（即R∪F ⊧ α）；否则返回“否”。</span></p></li></ol><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>注意：由于基化后的规则集是有限的，且S是命题公式的有限集合，因此不可满足性是可判定的（尽管可能是指数时间的）。</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>因此，该算法解决了D-ENTAILMENT问题。</span></p></blockquote><br/><h3><span>问题1.6：D-ENTAILMENT算法详解</span></h3><h4><span>问题定义</span></h4><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>D-ENTAILMENT问题是：给定一个有限的析取规则集合 </span><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi mathvariant="script">R</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathcal{R}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathcal">R</span></span></span></span><span>，一个有限的基事实集合 </span><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi mathvariant="script">F</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathcal{F}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathcal" style="margin-right:0.09931em;">F</span></span></span></span><span>，和一个无函数符号的基原子 </span><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>α</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\alpha</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.4306em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.0037em;">α</span></span></span></span><span>，我们需要判断是否 </span><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi mathvariant="script">R</mi><mo>∪</mo><mi mathvariant="script">F</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathcal{R} \cup \mathcal{F}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathcal">R</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">∪</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathcal" style="margin-right:0.09931em;">F</span></span></span></span><span> 的每一个模型都是 </span><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>α</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\alpha</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.4306em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.0037em;">α</span></span></span></span><span> 的模型。</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>换句话说，就是判断 </span><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi mathvariant="script">R</mi><mo>∪</mo><mi mathvariant="script">F</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathcal{R} \cup \mathcal{F}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathcal">R</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">∪</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathcal" style="margin-right:0.09931em;">F</span></span></span></span><span> 是否逻辑蕴含 </span><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>α</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\alpha</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.4306em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.0037em;">α</span></span></span></span><span>，记作 </span><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi mathvariant="script">R</mi><mo>∪</mo><mi mathvariant="script">F</mi><mo>⊨</mo><mi>α</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathcal{R} \cup \mathcal{F} \models \alpha</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathcal">R</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">∪</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.999em;vertical-align:-0.249em;"></span><span class="mord mathcal" style="margin-right:0.09931em;">F</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">⊨</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.4306em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.0037em;">α</span></span></span></span><span>。</span></p><h4><span>算法核心思想</span></h4><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>这个算法的核心思想是将一阶逻辑的蕴含问题转化为命题逻辑的不可满足性问题。具体来说：</span></p><ul><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><strong><span>逻辑等价转换</span></strong><span>：</span><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi mathvariant="script">R</mi><mo>∪</mo><mi mathvariant="script">F</mi><mo>⊨</mo><mi>α</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathcal{R} \cup \mathcal{F} \models \alpha</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathcal">R</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">∪</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.999em;vertical-align:-0.249em;"></span><span class="mord mathcal" style="margin-right:0.09931em;">F</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">⊨</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.4306em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.0037em;">α</span></span></span></span><span> 当且仅当 </span><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi mathvariant="script">R</mi><mo>∪</mo><mi mathvariant="script">F</mi><mo>∪</mo><mo stretchy="false">{</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">¬</mi><mi>α</mi><mo stretchy="false">}</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathcal{R} \cup \mathcal{F} \cup \{\neg \alpha\}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathcal">R</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">∪</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathcal" style="margin-right:0.09931em;">F</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">∪</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:1em;vertical-align:-0.25em;"></span><span class="mopen">{</span><span class="mord">¬</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.0037em;">α</span><span class="mclose">}</span></span></span></span><span> 是不可满足的</span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><strong><span>有限性保证</span></strong><span>：由于规则是无函数符号的，赫尔布朗宇宙是有限的，因此可以将一阶逻辑公式转化为命题逻辑公式</span></p></li></ul><h4><span>算法步骤详解</span></h4><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><strong><span>步骤1：确定赫尔布朗域</span></strong></p><ul><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>收集 </span><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi mathvariant="script">F</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathcal{F}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathcal" style="margin-right:0.09931em;">F</span></span></span></span><span> 和 </span><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi mathvariant="script">R</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathcal{R}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathcal">R</span></span></span></span><span> 中出现的所有常量符号，组成集合 </span><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>C</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">C</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.07153em;">C</span></span></span></span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>如果 </span><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>C</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">C</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.07153em;">C</span></span></span></span><span> 为空（即没有任何常量），则引入一个虚拟常量 </span><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>c</mi><mn>0</mn></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">c_0</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.5806em;vertical-align:-0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">c</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.3011em;"><span style="top:-2.55em;margin-left:0em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight">0</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><em><span>为什么需要这一步？</span></em><span> 因为后续的实例化步骤需要至少一个常量来替换变量</span></p></li></ul><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><strong><span>步骤2：实例化规则</span></strong></p><ul><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>对于 </span><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi mathvariant="script">R</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathcal{R}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathcal">R</span></span></span></span><span> 中的每条规则 </span><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>r</mi><mo>=</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">∀</mi><msub><mi>x</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo>…</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">∀</mi><msub><mi>x</mi><mi>k</mi></msub><mi mathvariant="normal">.</mi><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi>P</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo>∧</mo><mo>…</mo><mo>∧</mo><msub><mi>P</mi><mi>n</mi></msub><mo>→</mo><msub><mi>Q</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo>∨</mo><mo>…</mo><mo>∨</mo><msub><mi>Q</mi><mi>m</mi></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">r = \forall x_1 \ldots \forall x_k . (P_1 \wedge \ldots \wedge P_n \rightarrow Q_1 \vee \ldots \vee Q_m)</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.4306em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.02778em;">r</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:1em;vertical-align:-0.25em;"></span><span class="mord">∀</span><span class="mord"><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.1667em;"></span><span class="minner">…</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.1667em;"></span><span class="mord">∀</span><span class="mord"><span style="margin-right:0.13889em;">P</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.1514em;"><span style="top:-2.55em;margin-left:-0.1389em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">n</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="height:0.8778em;vertical-align:-0.1944em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">Q</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.3011em;"><span style="top:-2.55em;margin-left:0em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight">1</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="margin-right:0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.5556em;"></span><span class="minner">…</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">∨</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:1em;vertical-align:-0.25em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">Q</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.1514em;"><span style="top:-2.55em;margin-left:0em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">m</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose">)</span></span></span></span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>用 </span><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>C</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">C</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.07153em;">C</span></span></span></span><span> 中常量的所有可能组合替换变量 </span><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>x</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo separator="true">,</mo><mo>…</mo><mo separator="true">,</mo><msub><mi>x</mi><mi>k</mi></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">x_1, \ldots, x_k</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.625em;vertical-align:-0.1944em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">x</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.3011em;"><span style="top:-2.55em;margin-left:0em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight">1</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.1667em;"></span><span class="minner">…</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.1667em;"></span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.1667em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">x</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.3361em;"><span style="top:-2.55em;margin-left:0em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right:0.03148em;">k</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span>，生成所有基实例</span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>得到基规则集合 </span><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>G</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">G</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">G</span></span></span></span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><em><span>为什么可以这样做？</span></em><span> 因为无函数符号，所以赫尔布朗宇宙是有限的，实例化后的规则集合也是有限的</span></p></li></ul><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><strong><span>步骤3：构造测试集合</span></strong></p><ul><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>令 </span><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>S</mi><mo>=</mo><mi>G</mi><mo>∪</mo><mi mathvariant="script">F</mi><mo>∪</mo><mo stretchy="false">{</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">¬</mi><mi>α</mi><mo stretchy="false">}</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">S = G \cup \mathcal{F} \cup \{\neg \alpha\}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.05764em;">S</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">G</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">∪</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathcal" style="margin-right:0.09931em;">F</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">∪</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:1em;vertical-align:-0.25em;"></span><span class="mopen">{</span><span class="mord">¬</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.0037em;">α</span><span class="mclose">}</span></span></span></span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>这里 </span><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">¬</mi><mi>α</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\neg \alpha</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.4306em;"></span><span class="mord">¬</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.0037em;">α</span></span></span></span><span> 是 </span><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>α</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\alpha</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.4306em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.0037em;">α</span></span></span></span><span> 的否定</span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><em><span>为什么这样构造？</span></em><span> 我们要测试 </span><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi mathvariant="script">R</mi><mo>∪</mo><mi mathvariant="script">F</mi><mo>∪</mo><mo stretchy="false">{</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">¬</mi><mi>α</mi><mo stretchy="false">}</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathcal{R} \cup \mathcal{F} \cup \{\neg \alpha\}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathcal">R</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">∪</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathcal" style="margin-right:0.09931em;">F</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">∪</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:1em;vertical-align:-0.25em;"></span><span class="mopen">{</span><span class="mord">¬</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.0037em;">α</span><span class="mclose">}</span></span></span></span><span> 是否不可满足</span></p></li></ul><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><strong><span>步骤4：检查不可满足性</span></strong></p><ul><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>检查 </span><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>S</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">S</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.05764em;">S</span></span></span></span><span> 是否不可满足（即没有模型能满足 </span><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>S</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">S</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.05764em;">S</span></span></span></span><span> 中的所有公式）</span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>如果 </span><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>S</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">S</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.05764em;">S</span></span></span></span><span> 不可满足，返回 true（表示 </span><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi mathvariant="script">R</mi><mo>∪</mo><mi mathvariant="script">F</mi><mo>⊨</mo><mi>α</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathcal{R} \cup \mathcal{F} \models \alpha</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathcal">R</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">∪</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.999em;vertical-align:-0.249em;"></span><span class="mord mathcal" style="margin-right:0.09931em;">F</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">⊨</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.4306em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.0037em;">α</span></span></span></span><span>）</span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>如果 </span><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>S</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">S</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.05764em;">S</span></span></span></span><span> 可满足，返回 false（表示 </span><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi mathvariant="script">R</mi><mo>∪</mo><mi mathvariant="script">F</mi><mo>⊭</mo><mi>α</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathcal{R} \cup \mathcal{F} \not\models \alpha</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathcal">R</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">∪</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.8889em;vertical-align:-0.1944em;"></span><span class="mord mathcal" style="margin-right:0.09931em;">F</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel"><span class="mord vbox"><span class="thinbox"><span class="rlap"><span class="strut" style="height:0.8889em;vertical-align:-0.1944em;"></span><span class="inner"><span class="mord"><span class="mrel"></span></span></span><span class="fix"></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.999em;vertical-align:-0.249em;"></span><span class="mrel">⊨</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.4306em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.0037em;">α</span></span></span></span><span>）</span></p></li></ul><h4><span>算法正确性证明</span></h4><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><strong><span>为什么这个算法是正确的？</span></strong></p><ol start="1"><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><strong><span>有限性保证</span></strong><span>：由于规则是无函数符号的，实例化后的规则集合 </span><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>G</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">G</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">G</span></span></span></span><span> 是有限的，因此 </span><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>S</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">S</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.05764em;">S</span></span></span></span><span> 是一个有限的命题逻辑公式集合</span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><strong><span>语义等价性</span></strong><span>：</span></p><ul><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi mathvariant="script">R</mi><mo>∪</mo><mi mathvariant="script">F</mi><mo>⊨</mo><mi>α</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathcal{R} \cup \mathcal{F} \models \alpha</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathcal">R</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">∪</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.999em;vertical-align:-0.249em;"></span><span class="mord mathcal" style="margin-right:0.09931em;">F</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">⊨</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.4306em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.0037em;">α</span></span></span></span><span> 当且仅当 </span><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi mathvariant="script">R</mi><mo>∪</mo><mi mathvariant="script">F</mi><mo>∪</mo><mo stretchy="false">{</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">¬</mi><mi>α</mi><mo stretchy="false">}</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathcal{R} \cup \mathcal{F} \cup \{\neg \alpha\}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathcal">R</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">∪</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathcal" style="margin-right:0.09931em;">F</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">∪</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:1em;vertical-align:-0.25em;"></span><span class="mopen">{</span><span class="mord">¬</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.0037em;">α</span><span class="mclose">}</span></span></span></span><span> 不可满足</span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>这是逻辑学中的基本定理：一个公式集合蕴含另一个公式，当且仅当该公式集合与目标公式的否定一起构成矛盾</span></p></li></ul></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><strong><span>完备性</span></strong><span>：命题逻辑的不可满足性问题是可判定的，虽然可能需要指数时间，但题目不要求算法高效</span></p></li></ol><h4><span>实例说明</span></h4><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>假设：</span></p><ul><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi mathvariant="script">F</mi><mo>=</mo><mo stretchy="false">{</mo><mi>P</mi><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>a</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>Q</mi><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>b</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo stretchy="false">}</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathcal{F} = \{P(a), Q(b)\}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathcal" style="margin-right:0.09931em;">F</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:1em;vertical-align:-0.25em;"></span><span class="mopen">{</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.13889em;">P</span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathnormal">a</span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.1667em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">Q</span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathnormal">b</span><span class="mclose">)}</span></span></span></span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi mathvariant="script">R</mi><mo>=</mo><mo stretchy="false">{</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">∀</mi><mi>x</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">.</mi><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>P</mi><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>x</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo>→</mo><mi>R</mi><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>x</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo>∨</mo><mi>S</mi><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>x</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo stretchy="false">}</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathcal{R} = \{\forall x . (P(x) \rightarrow R(x) \vee S(x))\}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathcal">R</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:1em;vertical-align:-0.25em;"></span><span class="mopen">{</span><span class="mord">∀</span><span class="mord mathnormal">x</span><span class="mord">.</span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.13889em;">P</span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathnormal">x</span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">→</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:1em;vertical-align:-0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.00773em;">R</span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathnormal">x</span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">∨</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:1em;vertical-align:-0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.05764em;">S</span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathnormal">x</span><span class="mclose">))}</span></span></span></span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>α</mi><mo>=</mo><mi>R</mi><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>a</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\alpha = R(a)</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.4306em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.0037em;">α</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:1em;vertical-align:-0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.00773em;">R</span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathnormal">a</span><span class="mclose">)</span></span></span></span></p></li></ul><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><strong><span>步骤1</span></strong><span>：赫尔布朗域 </span><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>C</mi><mo>=</mo><mo stretchy="false">{</mo><mi>a</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>b</mi><mo stretchy="false">}</mo></mrow><annotation class="mclose">}</span></span></span></span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><strong><span>步骤2</span></strong><span>：实例化规则：</span></p><ul><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>当 </span><span class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>这个算法虽然简单，但理论上完备，能够正确解决 D-ENTAILMENT 问题。</span></p>

### 用户

根据提供的作业文件，我将逐一解答每个问题，提供详细的数学推导和解析。答案将使用英文撰写，以确保与问题描述的一致性。

### Problem 1.1

Consider the propositional logic formulas:
- \(\alpha = (\text{Alarm\_Rings} \rightarrow \text{Burglary}) \rightarrow (\text{Alarm\_Rings} \vee \neg \text{Burglary})\)
- \(\beta = (\text{Alarm\_Rings} \rightarrow \text{Burglary}) \rightarrow (\text{Alarm\_Rings} \wedge \text{Dog\_Barks} \rightarrow \text{Burglary})\)

#### 1. Write down all subformulas of \(\beta\).

The subformulas of \(\beta\) are:
- \(\text{Alarm\_Rings}\)
- \(\text{Burglary}\)
- \(\text{Dog\_Barks}\)
- \((\text{Alarm\_Rings} \rightarrow \text{Burglary})\)
- \((\text{Alarm\_Rings} \wedge \text{Dog\_Barks})\)
- \((\text{Alarm\_Rings} \wedge \text{Dog\_Barks} \rightarrow \text{Burglary})\)
- \(\beta\) itself

#### 2. How many interpretations are there for \(\alpha\) and for \(\beta\)?

- \(\alpha\) has 2 propositional variables (\(\text{Alarm\_Rings}\) and \(\text{Burglary}\)), so there are \(2^2 = 4\) interpretations.
- \(\beta\) has 3 propositional variables (\(\text{Alarm\_Rings}\), \(\text{Burglary}\), and \(\text{Dog\_Barks}\)), so there are \(2^3 = 8\) interpretations.

#### 3. Let \(\mathcal{I}\) be the interpretation for \(\alpha\) mapping \(\text{Alarm\_Rings}\) to true and \(\text{Burglary}\) to false. Apply the formula evaluation algorithm to determine whether \(\mathcal{I}\) is a model of \(\alpha\).

Evaluate \(\alpha\) under \(\mathcal{I}\):
- \(\text{Alarm\_Rings} = \text{true}\), \(\text{Burglary} = \text{false}\)
- Compute \(\text{Alarm\_Rings} \rightarrow \text{Burglary}\): \(\text{true} \rightarrow \text{false} = \text{false}\)
- Compute \(\text{Alarm\_Rings} \vee \neg \text{Burglary}\): \(\text{true} \vee \neg \text{false} = \text{true} \vee \text{true} = \text{true}\)
- Compute \(\alpha\): \((\text{false}) \rightarrow (\text{true}) = \text{true}\)
Thus, \(\mathcal{I}\) is a model of \(\alpha\).

#### 4. Let \(\mathcal{I}^{\prime}\) be the interpretation for \(\beta\) mapping all the propositional letters in \(\beta\) to true. Apply the formula evaluation algorithm to determine whether \(\mathcal{I}^{\prime}\) is a model of \(\beta\).

Evaluate \(\beta\) under \(\mathcal{I}^{\prime}\):
- \(\text{Alarm\_Rings} = \text{true}\), \(\text{Burglary} = \text{true}\), \(\text{Dog\_Barks} = \text{true}\)
- Compute \(\text{Alarm\_Rings} \rightarrow \text{Burglary}\): \(\text{true} \rightarrow \text{true} = \text{true}\)
- Compute \(\text{Alarm\_Rings} \wedge \text{Dog\_Barks}\): \(\text{true} \wedge \text{true} = \text{true}\)
- Compute \((\text{Alarm\_Rings} \wedge \text{Dog\_Barks}) \rightarrow \text{Burglary}\): \(\text{true} \rightarrow \text{true} = \text{true}\)
- Compute \(\beta\): \((\text{true}) \rightarrow (\text{true}) = \text{true}\)
Thus, \(\mathcal{I}^{\prime}\) is a model of \(\beta\).

#### 5. Is \(\alpha\) valid?

No, \(\alpha\) is not valid. A counterexample is when \(\text{Alarm\_Rings} = \text{false}\) and \(\text{Burglary} = \text{true}\):
- Compute \(\text{Alarm\_Rings} \rightarrow \text{Burglary}\): \(\text{false} \rightarrow \text{true} = \text{true}\)
- Compute \(\text{Alarm\_Rings} \vee \neg \text{Burglary}\): \(\text{false} \vee \neg \text{true} = \text{false} \vee \text{false} = \text{false}\)
- Compute \(\alpha\): \(\text{true} \rightarrow \text{false} = \text{false}\)
Thus, \(\alpha\) is false in this interpretation, so it is not valid.

### Problem 1.2

Formalize the statements using propositional logic with the following atoms:
- \(S4\): The tumour is Stage 4
- \(M\): The tumour exhibits metastasis
- \(B\): The tumour is benign
- \(G\): The tumour has a good prognosis
- \(H\): The tumour has a high survival rate
- \(L\): The tumour has a low survival rate

Knowledge base \(\text{KB}\):
1. \(S4 \rightarrow M\)
2. \(\neg S4 \rightarrow (\neg M \wedge B)\)
3. \(B \rightarrow G\) (from "if benign, then good prognosis")
4. \(G \rightarrow H\) (from "if good prognosis, then high survival rate")
5. \(H \leftrightarrow \neg L\) (from "high survival rate iff not low survival rate")

#### Does your formalisation entail that, if the tumour is Stage 4, then it has low survival rate?

Check if \(\text{KB} \models S4 \rightarrow L\):
- Consider a model where \(S4 = \text{true}\), \(M = \text{true}\), \(B = \text{false}\), \(G = \text{false}\), \(H = \text{false}\), \(L = \text{true}\).
- Verify \(\text{KB}\):
  - \(S4 \rightarrow M\): \(\text{true} \rightarrow \text{true} = \text{true}\)
  - \(\neg S4 \rightarrow (\neg M \wedge B)\): \(\text{false} \rightarrow \ldots = \text{true}\)
  - \(B \rightarrow G\): \(\text{false} \rightarrow \text{false} = \text{true}\)
  - \(G \rightarrow H\): \(\text{false} \rightarrow \text{false} = \text{true}\)
  - \(H \leftrightarrow \neg L\): \(\text{false} \leftrightarrow \text{false} = \text{true}\)
- So \(\text{KB}\) is satisfied, but \(S4 \rightarrow L\) is \(\text{true} \rightarrow \text{true} = \text{true}\) in this model. However, to disprove entailment, we need a model where \(\text{KB}\) is true but \(S4 \rightarrow L\) is false. For \(S4 \rightarrow L\) to be false, \(S4\) must be true and \(L\) false.
- Consider another model: \(S4 = \text{true}\), \(M = \text{true}\), \(B = \text{true}\), \(G = \text{true}\), \(H = \text{true}\), \(L = \text{false}\).
- Verify \(\text{KB}\):
  - \(S4 \rightarrow M\): \(\text{true} \rightarrow \text{true} = \text{true}\)
  - \(\neg S4 \rightarrow (\neg M \wedge B)\): \(\text{false} \rightarrow \ldots = \text{true}\)
  - \(B \rightarrow G\): \(\text{true} \rightarrow \text{true} = \text{true}\)
  - \(G \rightarrow H\): \(\text{true} \rightarrow \text{true} = \text{true}\)
  - \(H \leftrightarrow \neg L\): \(\text{true} \leftrightarrow \text{true} = \text{true}\)
- So \(\text{KB}\) is satisfied, but \(S4 \rightarrow L\) is \(\text{true} \rightarrow \text{false} = \text{false}\). Thus, \(\text{KB} \not\models S4 \rightarrow L\).

#### Does your formalisation entail that, if it is not Stage 4, then it has a good prognosis?

Check if \(\text{KB} \models \neg S4 \rightarrow G\):
- From \(\text{KB}\), \(\neg S4 \rightarrow (\neg M \wedge B)\) and \(B \rightarrow G\).
- If \(\neg S4\) is true, then \(\neg M \wedge B\) is true, so \(B\) is true, and thus \(G\) is true.
- Therefore, \(\neg S4 \rightarrow G\) is true in all models of \(\text{KB}\), so \(\text{KB} \models \neg S4 \rightarrow G\).

### Problem 1.3

First-order logic knowledge base \(\mathcal{K}\) using the given predicates:

1. \(\forall x \, (\text{VSD}(x) \rightarrow \text{CHD}(x))\)
2. \(\forall x \, (\text{AS}(x) \rightarrow \text{CHD}(x))\)
3. \(\forall x \, (\text{VSD}(x) \rightarrow \exists y \, (\text{Septum}(y) \wedge \text{affects}(x,y)))\)
4. \(\forall x \, (\text{Septum}(x) \rightarrow \text{Tissue}(x) \wedge \exists y \, (\text{LHeart}(y) \wedge \text{partOf}(x,y)) \wedge \exists z \, (\text{RHeart}(z) \wedge \text{partOf}(x,z)))\)
5. \(\forall x \, (\text{Heart}(x) \rightarrow \text{Organ}(x))\)
6. \(\exists x \, (\text{GATA4}(x) \wedge \text{Gene}(x) \wedge \exists y \, (\text{VSD}(y) \wedge \text{relatedTo}(x,y)))\)
7. \(\forall x \, (\text{AS}(x) \rightarrow \exists y \, (\text{Heart}(y) \wedge \text{suffersCondition}(y,x) \wedge \exists z \, (\text{TrieValve}(z) \wedge \text{partOf}(z,y) \wedge \text{hasDisPart}(y,z))))\)
8. \(\forall x \, (\text{Heart}(x) \wedge \exists y \, (\text{TrieValve}(y) \wedge \text{partOf}(y,x) \wedge \text{hasDisPart}(x,y)) \rightarrow \exists z \, (\text{CHD}(z) \wedge \text{suffersCondition}(x,z)))\)
9. \(\forall x \forall y \forall z \, (\text{partOf}(x,y) \wedge \text{partOf}(y,z) \wedge \text{Organ}(z) \rightarrow \text{partOf}(x,z))\)
10. \(\forall x \, (\text{CHD}(x) \rightarrow \forall y \, (\text{affects}(x,y) \rightarrow \exists z \, (\text{Heart}(z) \wedge \text{partOf}(y,z))))\)
11. \(\exists x \, (\text{Murmur}(x) \wedge \exists y \, (\text{CHD}(y) \wedge \text{symptomOf}(x,y)))\)
12. \(\exists x \, (\text{Murmur}(x) \wedge \neg \exists y \, (\text{CHD}(y) \wedge \text{symptomOf}(x,y)))\)
13. \(\forall x \, (\text{Auscultation}(x) \rightarrow \text{MedProc}(x) \wedge \neg \text{SurProc}(x))\)

Note: Axiom 12 captures "not all heart murmurs are caused by congenital heart defects". Axiom 13 defines auscultation as a non-surgical medical procedure. No explicit axiom is needed for statement 12 as it is logically inherent.

### Problem 1.4

Datalog rules for familial relationships:

- \(\text{Father}(x,y) \leftarrow \text{Parent}(x,y), \text{Male}(x)\)
- \(\text{Mother}(x,y) \leftarrow \text{Parent}(x,y), \text{Female}(x)\)
- \(\text{Son}(x,y) \leftarrow \text{Parent}(y,x), \text{Male}(x)\)
- \(\text{Daughter}(x,y) \leftarrow \text{Parent}(y,x), \text{Female}(x)\)
- \(\text{Sibling}(x,y) \leftarrow \text{Parent}(z,x), \text{Parent}(z,y), x \neq y\)
- \(\text{Brother}(x,y) \leftarrow \text{Sibling}(x,y), \text{Male}(x)\)
- \(\text{Sister}(x,y) \leftarrow \text{Sibling}(x,y), \text{Female}(x)\)
- \(\text{Grandparent}(x,y) \leftarrow \text{Parent}(x,z), \text{Parent}(z,y)\)
- \(\text{Uncle}(x,y) \leftarrow \text{Parent}(z,y), \text{Brother}(x,z)\)
- \(\text{Cousin}(x,y) \leftarrow \text{Parent}(a,x), \text{Parent}(b,y), \text{Sibling}(a,b)\)

**Expressivity limitations**: Datalog cannot directly express negative conditions or existential quantification in the head. For example, defining "x has no children" requires negation, which is not supported in pure Datalog without safe negation. Also, relationships like "step-sibling" or "half-sibling" may require additional rules or predicates not covered here.

### Problem 1.5

Datalog knowledge base \(\mathcal{K} = \langle \mathcal{R}, \mathcal{F} \rangle\):
- \(\mathcal{F} = \{\text{Father}(john, mary), \text{Mother}(mary, peter), \text{Father}(john, david)\}\)
- \(\mathcal{R} = \{
    \text{Parent}(x,y) \wedge \text{Parent}(y,z) \rightarrow \text{GrandParent}(x,z), \\
    \text{Parent}(x,y) \wedge \text{Parent}(x,z) \rightarrow \text{Sibling}(y,z), \\
    \text{Father}(x,y) \rightarrow \text{Parent}(x,y), \\
    \text{Mother}(x,y) \rightarrow \text{Parent}(x,y)
\}\)

#### 1. Using backward chaining, show that John is a grandparent of Peter.

Backward chaining for \(\text{GrandParent}(john, peter)\):
- Goal: \(\text{GrandParent}(john, peter)\)
- Match with rule: \(\text{GrandParent}(x,z) \leftarrow \text{Parent}(x,y), \text{Parent}(y,z)\)
- Unify \(x = john\), \(z = peter\), so subgoals: \(\text{Parent}(john,y)\) and \(\text{Parent}(y,peter)\)
- Solve \(\text{Parent}(john,y)\): from \(\text{Father}(john, mary)\) and rule \(\text{Father}(x,y) \rightarrow \text{Parent}(x,y)\), derive \(\text{Parent}(john, mary)\), so \(y = mary\)
- Solve \(\text{Parent}(mary,peter)\): from \(\text{Mother}(mary, peter)\) and rule \(\text{Mother}(x,y) \rightarrow \text{Parent}(x,y)\), derive \(\text{Parent}(mary, peter)\)
- Thus, \(\text{GrandParent}(john, peter)\) is derived.

#### 2. Using forward-chaining, show that Mary and David are siblings.

Forward chaining:
- Facts: \(\text{Father}(john, mary)\), \(\text{Mother}(mary, peter)\), \(\text{Father}(john, david)\)
- Apply rule \(\text{Father}(x,y) \rightarrow \text{Parent}(x,y)\):
  - \(\text{Parent}(john, mary)\) from \(\text{Father}(john, mary)\)
  - \(\text{Parent}(john, david)\) from \(\text{Father}(john, david)\)
- Apply rule \(\text{Mother}(x,y) \rightarrow \text{Parent}(x,y)\):
  - \(\text{Parent}(mary, peter)\) from \(\text{Mother}(mary, peter)\)
- Apply rule \(\text{Parent}(x,y) \wedge \text{Parent}(x,z) \rightarrow \text{Sibling}(y,z)\):
  - With \(x = john\), \(y = mary\), \(z = david\), we have \(\text{Parent}(john, mary)\) and \(\text{Parent}(john, david)\), so derive \(\text{Sibling}(mary, david)\)

### Problem 1.6

The D-ENTAILMENT problem is defined for a finite set of disjunctive rules \(\mathcal{R}\), a finite set of ground facts \(\mathcal{F}\), and a function-free ground atom \(\alpha\). The answer is true iff every model of \(\mathcal{R} \cup \mathcal{F}\) is a model of \(\alpha\).

**Algorithm**:
1. Let \(C\) be the set of all constants appearing in \(\mathcal{F}\) and \(\mathcal{R}\). If no constants exist, introduce a dummy constant to ensure grounding.
2. Ground all rules in \(\mathcal{R}\) by replacing all variables with constants from \(C\), resulting in a set of ground rules \(G\).
3. Let \(S = G \cup \mathcal{F} \cup \{\neg \alpha\}\).
4. Check if \(S\) is unsatisfiable (i.e., no model satisfies \(S\)).
   - If yes, return true (every model of \(\mathcal{R} \cup \mathcal{F}\) satisfies \(\alpha\)).
   - If no, return false (there exists a model of \(\mathcal{R} \cup \mathcal{F}\) that does not satisfy \(\alpha\)).

This algorithm solves D-ENTAILMENT by reducing it to propositional unsatisfiability checking. Since the Herbrand universe is finite (no function symbols), grounding is finite, and propositional satisfiability is decidable.把这个答案翻译成中文

---

### DeepSeek AI

<p>思考：</p><blockquote><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>我们首先将问题1.1到1.6的答案翻译成中文。注意，保持数学公式和逻辑符号的完整性，同时将解释和步骤用中文表述。</span></p><h3><span>问题1.1</span></h3><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>考虑以下命题逻辑公式：</span></p><ul><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>α</mi><mo>=</mo><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mtext>Alarm_Rings</mtext><mo>→</mo><mtext>Burglary</mtext><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo>→</mo><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mtext>Alarm_Rings</mtext><mo>∨</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">¬</mi><mtext>Burglary</mtext><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\alpha = (\text{Alarm\_Rings} \rightarrow \text{Burglary}) \rightarrow (\text{Alarm\_Rings} \vee \neg \text{Burglary})</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.4306em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.0037em;">α</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:1.06em;vertical-align:-0.31em;"></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">Alarm_Rings</span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">→</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:1em;vertical-align:-0.25em;"></span><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">Burglary</span></span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">→</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:1.06em;vertical-align:-0.31em;"></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">Alarm_Rings</span></span><span class="mspace" stretchy="false">)</mo><mo>→</mo><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mtext>Alarm_Rings</mtext><mo>∧</mo><mtext>Dog_Barks</mtext><mo>→</mo><mtext>Burglary</mtext><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><annotation </span><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>α</mi></mrow><annotation 有2个命题变量（</span><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mtext>Alarm_Rings</mtext></mrow><annotation </span><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mtext>Alarm_Rings</mtext></mrow><annotation 的模型。</span></h4><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>在解释 </span><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi \text{true}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:1.0044em;vertical-align:-0.31em;"></span><span \text{false}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.8889em;vertical-align:-0.1944em;"></span><span class="vlist" style="height:0.7519em;"><span style="top:-3.063em;margin-right:0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height:2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight">′</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span> 是 </span><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>β</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\beta</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.8889em;vertical-align:-0.1944em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.05278em;">β</span></span></span></span><span> 的模型。</span></p></li></ul><h4><span>5. </span><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>α</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\alpha</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.4306em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.0037em;">α</span></span></span></span><span> 是有效的吗？</span></h4><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>不，</span><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>α</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\alpha</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.4306em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.0037em;">α</span></span></span></span><span> 不是有效的。反例是当 </span><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mtext>Alarm_Rings</mtext><mo>=</mo><mtext>false</mtext></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\text{Alarm\_Rings} = \text{false}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:1.0044em;vertical-align:-0.31em;"></span><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">Alarm_Rings</span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6944em;"></span><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">false</span></span></span></span></span><span> 且 </span><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mtext>Burglary</mtext><mo>=</mo><mtext>true</mtext></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\text{Burglary} = \text{true}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.8889em;vertical-align:-0.1944em;"></span><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">Burglary</span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6151em;"></span><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">true</span></span></span></span></span><span>：</span></p><ul><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>计算 </span><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mtext>Alarm_Rings</mtext><mo>→</mo><mtext>Burglary</mtext></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\text{Alarm\_Rings} \rightarrow \text{Burglary}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:1.0044em;vertical-align:-0.31em;"></span><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">Alarm_Rings</span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">→</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.8889em;vertical-align:-0.1944em;"></span><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">Burglary</span></span></span></span></span><span>：</span><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mtext>false</mtext><mo>→</mo><mtext>true</mtext><mo>=</mo><mtext>true</mtext></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\text{false} \rightarrow \text{true} = \text{true}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6944em;"></span><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">false</span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">→</span><span class="mspace" style="height:0.6151em;"></span><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">true</span></span></span></span></span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>计算 </span><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mtext>Alarm_Rings</mtext><mo>∨</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">¬</mi><mtext>Burglary</mtext></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\text{Alarm\_Rings} \vee \neg \text{Burglary}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:1.0044em;vertical-align:-0.31em;"></span><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">Alarm_Rings</span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">∨</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="mord">Burglary</span></span></span></span></span><span>：</span><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mtext>false</mtext><mo>∨</mo><mi \vee \neg \text{true} = \text{false} \vee \text{false} = \text{false}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6944em;"></span><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">false</span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">∨</span><span class="mspace" class="mord">true</span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6944em;"></span><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">false</span></span></span></span></span></p></li><li><p encoding="application/x-tex">\alpha</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.4306em;"></span><span \rightarrow \text{false} = \text{false}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6151em;"></span><span style="margin-right:0.0037em;">α</span></span></span></span><span> 为假，所以它不是有效的。</span></p></li></ul><h3><span>问题1.2</span></h3><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>使用以下原子进行命题逻辑形式化：</span></p><ul><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">G</span></span></span></span><span>：肿瘤预后良好</span></p></li><li><p class="mord mathnormal">L</span></span></span></span><span>（从“高存活率当且仅当不是低存活率”）</span></p></li></ol><h4><span>你的形式化是否蕴含：如果肿瘤是4期，则它具有低存活率？</span></h4><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>检查 </span><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mtext>KB</mtext><mo>⊨</mo><mi>S</mi><mn>4</mn><mo>→</mo><mi>L</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\text{KB} \models S4 \rightarrow L</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.999em;vertical-align:-0.249em;"></span><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">KB</span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">⊨</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.05764em;">S</span><span class="mord">4</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">→</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">L</span></span></span></span><span>：</span></p><ul><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>考虑一个模型：</span><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>S</mi><mn>4</mn><mo>=</mo><mtext>true</mtext></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">S4 = \text{true}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.05764em;">S</span><span class="mord">4</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6151em;"></span><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">true</span></span></span></span></span><span>，</span><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>M</mi><mo>=</mo><mtext>true</mtext></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">M = \text{true}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.10903em;">M</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6151em;"></span><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">true</span></span></span></span></span><span>，</span><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>B</mi><mo>=</mo><mtext>false</mtext></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">B = \text{false}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" \rightarrow L</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.8889em;vertical-align:-0.1944em;"></span><span class="strut" style="height:0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">L</span></span></span></span><span>。</span></p></li></ul><h4><span>你的形式化是否蕴含：如果它不是4期，则它预后良好？</span></h4><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>检查 </span><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mtext>KB</mtext><mo>⊨</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">¬</mi><mi>S</mi><mn>4</mn><mo>→</mo><mi>G</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\text{KB} \models \neg S4 \rightarrow G</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.999em;vertical-align:-0.249em;"></span><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">KB</span></span><span style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">→</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">G</span></span></span></span><span>：</span></p><ul><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>从 </span><span class="katex"><span encoding="application/x-tex">\text{KB}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">KB</span></span></span></span></span><span>，</span><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">¬</mi><mi>S</mi><mn>4</mn><mo>→</mo><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">¬</mi><mi>M</mi><mo>∧</mo><mi>B</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\neg S4 \rightarrow (\neg M \wedge B)</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord">¬</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.05764em;">S</span><span class="mord">4</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">→</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:1em;vertical-align:-0.25em;"></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord">¬</span><span style="margin-right:0.05017em;">B</span><span class="mclose">)</span></span></span></span><span> 和 </span><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.05017em;">B</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">→</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">G</span></span></span></span><span>。</span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>如果 </span><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">¬</mi><mi>S</mi><mn>4</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\neg S4</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord">¬</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.05764em;">S</span><span class="mord">4</span></span></span></span><span> 为真，则 </span><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math B</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord">¬</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.10903em;">M</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">∧</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.05017em;">B</span></span></span></span><span> 为真，所以 </span><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>B</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">B</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.05017em;">B</span></span></span></span><span> 为真，因此 </span><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>G</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">G</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">G</span></span></span></span><span> 为真。</span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>因此，在所有满足 </span><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mtext>KB</mtext></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\text{KB}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">KB</span></span></span></span></span><span> 的模型中，</span><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">¬</mi><mi>S</mi><mn>4</mn><mo>→</mo><mi>G</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\neg S4 \rightarrow G</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord">¬</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.05764em;">S</span><span class="mord">4</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">→</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">G</span></span></span></span><span> 为真，所以 </span><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mtext>KB</mtext><mo>⊨</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">¬</mi><mi>S</mi><mn>4</mn><mo>→</mo><mi>G</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\text{KB} \models \neg S4 \rightarrow G</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.999em;vertical-align:-0.249em;"></span><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">KB</span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">⊨</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord">¬</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.05764em;">S</span><span class="mord">4</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">→</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">G</span></span></span></span><span>。</span></p></li></ul><h3><span>问题1.3</span></h3><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>使用给定的一阶逻辑谓词构建知识库 </span><span class="katex"><span class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>注意：公理12捕捉了“并非所有心脏杂音都是由先天性心脏缺陷引起的”。公理13将听诊定义为非手术医疗程序。对于陈述12，不需要显式公理，因为它在逻辑上是固有的。</span></p><h3><span>问题1.4</span></h3><p class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.1667em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.03588em;">y</span><span class="mclose">)</span><span
