mathnormal">a</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.1667em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">b</span><span class="mclose">)</span></span></span></span></p></li></ul><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><strong><span>表达性限制</span></strong><span>：Datalog不能直接表达否定条件或头部的存在量词。例如，定义“x没有孩子”需要否定，而纯Datalog不支持安全否定。此外，像“继兄弟姐妹”或“同父异母的兄弟姐妹”这样的关系可能需要此处未涵盖的额外规则或谓词。</span></p><h3><span>问题1.5</span></h3><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>Datalog知识库 </span><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi mathvariant="script">K</mi><mo>=</mo><mo stretchy="false">⟨</mo><mi mathvariant="script">R</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi mathvariant="script">F</mi><mo stretchy="false">⟩</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathcal{K} = \langle \mathcal{R}, \mathcal{F} \rangle</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathcal" style="margin-right:0.01445em;">K</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:1em;vertical-align:-0.25em;"></span><span class="mopen">⟨</span><span class="mord mathcal">R</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.1667em;"></span><span class="mord mathcal" style="margin-right:0.09931em;">F</span><span class="mclose">⟩</span></span></span></span><span>：</span></p><ul><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi mathvariant="script">F</mi><mo>=</mo><mo stretchy="false">{</mo><mtext>Father</mtext><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>j</mi><mi>o</mi><mi>h</mi><mi>n</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>m</mi><mi>a</mi><mi>r</mi><mi>y</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo separator="true">,</mo><mtext>Mother</mtext><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>m</mi><mi>a</mi><mi>r</mi><mi>y</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>p</mi><mi>e</mi><mi>t</mi><mi>e</mi><mi>r</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo separator="true">,</mo><mtext>Father</mtext><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>j</mi><mi>o</mi><mi>h</mi><mi>n</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>d</mi><mi>a</mi><mi>v</mi><mi>i</mi><mi>d</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo stretchy="false">}</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathcal{F} = \{\text{Father}(john, mary), \text{Mother}(mary, peter), \text{Father}(john, david)\}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathcal" style="margin-right:0.09931em;">F</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:1em;vertical-align:-0.25em;"></span><span class="mopen">{</span><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">Father</span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.05724em;">j</span><span class="mord mathnormal">o</span><span class="mord mathnormal">hn</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.1667em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">ma</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.03588em;">ry</span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.1667em;"></span><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">Mother</span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathnormal">ma</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.03588em;">ry</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.1667em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">p</span><span class="mord mathnormal">e</span><span class="mord mathnormal">t</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.02778em;">er</span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.1667em;"></span><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">Father</span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.05724em;">j</span><span class="mord mathnormal">o</span><span class="mord mathnormal">hn</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.1667em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">d</span><span class="mord mathnormal">a</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.03588em;">v</span><span class="mord mathnormal">i</span><span class="mord mathnormal">d</span><span class="mclose">)}</span></span></span></span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi mathvariant="script">R</mi><mo>=</mo><mo stretchy="false">{</mo><mtext>Parent</mtext><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>x</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>y</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo>∧</mo><mtext>Parent</mtext><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>y</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>z</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo>→</mo><mtext>GrandParent</mtext><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>x</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>z</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo separator="true">,</mo><mspace linebreak="newline"></mspace><mtext>Parent</mtext><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>x</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>y</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo>∧</mo><mtext>Parent</mtext><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>x</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>z</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo>→</mo><mtext>Sibling</mtext><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>y</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>z</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo separator="true">,</mo><mspace linebreak="newline"></mspace><mtext>Father</mtext><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>x</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>y</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo>→</mo><mtext>Parent</mtext><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>x</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>y</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo separator="true">,</mo><mspace linebreak="newline"></mspace><mtext>Mother</mtext><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>x</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>y</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo>→</mo><mtext>Parent</mtext><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>x</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>y</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo stretchy="false">}</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathcal{R} = \{
  \text{Parent}(x,y) \wedge \text{Parent}(y,z) \rightarrow \text{GrandParent}(x,z), \\
  \text{Parent}(x,y) \wedge \text{Parent}(x,z) \rightarrow \text{Sibling}(y,z), \\
  \text{Father}(x,y) \rightarrow \text{Parent}(x,y), \\
  \text{Mother}(x,y) \rightarrow \text{Parent}(x,y)
\}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathcal">R</span><span style="margin-right:0.1667em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.04398em;">z</span><span class="mclose">)</span></span></span></span><span>：</span></p><ul><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>取 </span><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>x</mi><mo>=</mo><mi>j</mi><mi>o</mi><mi>h</mi><mi>n</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">x = john</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.4306em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">x</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.8889em;vertical-align:-0.1944em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.05724em;">j</span><span class="mord mathnormal">o</span><span class="mord mathnormal">hn</span></span></span></span><span>，</span><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>y</mi><mo>=</mo><mi>m</mi><mi>a</mi><mi>r</mi><mi>y</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">y = mary</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.625em;vertical-align:-0.1944em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.03588em;">y</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.625em;vertical-align:-0.1944em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">ma</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.03588em;">ry</span></span></span></span><span>，</span><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>z</mi><mo>=</mo><mi>d</mi><mi>a</mi><mi>v</mi><mi>i</mi><mi>d</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">z = david</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.4306em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.04398em;">z</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6944em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">d</span><span class="mord mathnormal">a</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.03588em;">v</span><span class="mord mathnormal">i</span><span class="mord mathnormal">d</span></span></span></span><span>，我们有 </span><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mtext>Parent</mtext><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>j</mi><mi>o</mi><mi>h</mi><mi>n</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>m</mi><mi>a</mi><mi>r</mi><mi>y</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\text{Parent}(john, mary)</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:1em;vertical-align:-0.25em;"></span><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">Parent</span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.05724em;">j</span><span class="mord mathnormal">o</span><span class="mord mathnormal">hn</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.1667em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">ma</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.03588em;">ry</span><span class="mclose">)</span></span></span></span><span> 和 </span><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mtext>Parent</mtext><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>j</mi><mi>o</mi><mi>h</mi><mi>n</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>d</mi><mi>a</mi><mi>v</mi><mi>i</mi><mi>d</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\text{Parent}(john, david)</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:1em;vertical-align:-0.25em;"></span><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">Parent</span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.05724em;">j</span><span class="mord mathnormal">o</span><span class="mord mathnormal">hn</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.1667em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">d</span><span class="mord mathnormal">a</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.03588em;">v</span><span class="mord mathnormal">i</span><span class="mord mathnormal">d</span><span class="mclose">)</span></span></span></span><span>，因此推导出 </span><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mtext>Sibling</mtext><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>m</mi><mi>a</mi><mi>r</mi><mi>y</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>d</mi><mi>a</mi><mi>v</mi><mi>i</mi><mi>d</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\text{Sibling}(mary, david)</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:1em;vertical-align:-0.25em;"></span><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">Sibling</span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathnormal">ma</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.03588em;">ry</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.1667em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">d</span><span class="mord mathnormal">a</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.03588em;">v</span><span class="mord mathnormal">i</span><span class="mord mathnormal">d</span><span class="mclose">)</span></span></span></span></p></li></ul></li></ul><h3><span>问题1.6</span></h3><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>D-ENTAILMENT问题定义为：给定一个有限的析取规则集合 </span><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi mathvariant="script">R</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathcal{R}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathcal">R</span></span></span></span><span>，一个有限的基事实集合 </span><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi mathvariant="script">F</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathcal{F}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathcal" style="margin-right:0.09931em;">F</span></span></span></span><span>，和一个无函数符号的基原子 </span><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>α</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\alpha</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.4306em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.0037em;">α</span></span></span></span><span>。当且仅当 </span><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi mathvariant="script">R</mi><mo>∪</mo><mi mathvariant="script">F</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathcal{R} \cup \mathcal{F}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathcal">R</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">∪</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathcal" style="margin-right:0.09931em;">F</span></span></span></span><span> 的每个模型都是 </span><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>α</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\alpha</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.4306em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.0037em;">α</span></span></span></span><span> 的模型时，答案为真。</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><strong><span>算法</span></strong><span>：</span></p><ol start="1"><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>令 </span><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>C</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">C</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.07153em;">C</span></span></span></span><span> 为 </span><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi mathvariant="script">F</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathcal{F}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathcal" style="margin-right:0.09931em;">F</span></span></span></span><span> 和 </span><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi mathvariant="script">R</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathcal{R}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathcal">R</span></span></span></span><span> 中出现的所有常量的集合。如果没有常量，则引入一个虚拟常量以确保实例化。</span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>将 </span><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi mathvariant="script">R</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathcal{R}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathcal">R</span></span></span></span><span> 中的所有规则通过用 </span><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>C</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">C</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.07153em;">C</span></span></span></span><span> 中的常量替换所有变量进行实例化，得到基规则集合 </span><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>G</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">G</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">G</span></span></span></span><span>。</span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>令 </span><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>S</mi><mo>=</mo><mi>G</mi><mo>∪</mo><mi mathvariant="script">F</mi><mo>∪</mo><mo stretchy="false">{</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">¬</mi><mi>α</mi><mo stretchy="false">}</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">S = G \cup \mathcal{F} \cup \{\neg \alpha\}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.05764em;">S</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">G</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">∪</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathcal" style="margin-right:0.09931em;">F</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">∪</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:1em;vertical-align:-0.25em;"></span><span class="mopen">{</span><span class="mord">¬</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.0037em;">α</span><span class="mclose">}</span></span></span></span><span>。</span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>检查 </span><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>S</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">S</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.05764em;">S</span></span></span></span><span> 是否不可满足（即没有模型满足 </span><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>S</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">S</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.05764em;">S</span></span></span></span><span>）。</span></p><ul><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>如果是，返回 true（表示 </span><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi mathvariant="script">R</mi><mo>∪</mo><mi mathvariant="script">F</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathcal{R} \cup \mathcal{F}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathcal">R</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">∪</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathcal" style="margin-right:0.09931em;">F</span></span></span></span><span> 的每个模型都满足 </span><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>α</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\alpha</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.4306em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.0037em;">α</span></span></span></span><span>）。</span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>如果否，返回 false（表示存在 </span><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi mathvariant="script">R</mi><mo>∪</mo><mi mathvariant="script">F</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathcal{R} \cup \mathcal{F}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathcal">R</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">∪</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathcal" style="margin-right:0.09931em;">F</span></span></span></span><span> 的模型不满足 </span><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>α</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\alpha</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.4306em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.0037em;">α</span></span></span></span><span>）。</span></p></li></ul></li></ol><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>该算法通过将D-ENTAILMENT问题归约为命题不可满足性检查来解决问题。由于赫尔布朗宇宙是有限的（无函数符号），实例化是有限的，并且命题可满足性是可判定的。</span></p></blockquote><br/><h3><span>问题1.1</span></h3><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>考虑以下命题逻辑公式：</span></p><ul><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>α = (警报响起 → 入室盗窃) → (警报响起 ∨ ¬入室盗窃)</span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>β = (警报响起 → 入室盗窃) → (警报响起 ∧ 狗叫 → 入室盗窃)</span></p></li></ul><h4><span>1. 写出β的所有子公式</span></h4><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>β的子公式包括：</span></p><ul><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>警报响起</span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>入室盗窃</span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>狗叫</span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>(警报响起 → 入室盗窃)</span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>(警报响起 ∧ 狗叫)</span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>(警报响起 ∧ 狗叫 → 入室盗窃)</span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>β本身</span></p></li></ul><h4><span>2. α和β分别有多少种解释？</span></h4><ul><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>α有2个命题变量（警报响起和入室盗窃），因此有2² = 4种解释</span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>β有3个命题变量（警报响起、入室盗窃和狗叫），因此有2³ = 8种解释</span></p></li></ul><h4><span>3. 判断解释ℐ是否是α的模型</span></h4><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>在解释ℐ下：</span></p><ul><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>警报响起 = 真，入室盗窃 = 假</span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>计算警报响起 → 入室盗窃：真 → 假 = 假</span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>计算警报响起 ∨ ¬入室盗窃：真 ∨ 真 = 真</span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>计算α：假 → 真 = 真</span><br><span>因此，ℐ是α的模型。</span></p></li></ul><h4><span>4. 判断解释ℐ′是否是β的模型</span></h4><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>在解释ℐ′下：</span></p><ul><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>所有命题变量都为真</span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>计算警报响起 → 入室盗窃：真 → 真 = 真</span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>计算警报响起 ∧ 狗叫：真 ∧ 真 = 真</span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>计算(警报响起 ∧ 狗叫) → 入室盗窃：真 → 真 = 真</span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>计算β：真 → 真 = 真</span><br><span>因此，ℐ′是β的模型。</span></p></li></ul><h4><span>5. α是否有效？</span></h4><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>α不是有效的。反例：</span></p><ul><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>当警报响起 = 假，入室盗窃 = 真时</span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>计算警报响起 → 入室盗窃：假 → 真 = 真</span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>计算警报响起 ∨ ¬入室盗窃：假 ∨ 假 = 假</span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>计算α：真 → 假 = 假</span><br><span>因此，α在此解释下为假，不是有效公式。</span></p></li></ul><h3><span>问题1.2</span></h3><h4><span>知识库形式化</span></h4><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>使用以下命题变量：</span></p><ul><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>S4：肿瘤为4期</span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>M：肿瘤发生转移</span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>B：肿瘤是良性的</span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>G：肿瘤预后良好</span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>H：肿瘤具有高存活率</span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>L：肿瘤具有低存活率</span></p></li></ul><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>知识库KB：</span></p><ol start="1"><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>S4 → M</span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>¬S4 → (¬M ∧ B)</span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>B → G</span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>G → H</span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>H ↔ ¬L</span></p></li></ol><h4><span>是否蕴含：如果肿瘤是4期，则它具有低存活率？</span></h4><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>不蕴含。存在满足KB但不满足S4 → L的模型：</span></p><ul><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>S4 = 真，M = 真，B = 真，G = 真，H = 真，L = 假</span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>验证KB：</span></p><ul><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>S4 → M：真 → 真 = 真</span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>¬S4 → (¬M ∧ B)：假 → ... = 真</span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>B → G：真 → 真 = 真</span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>G → H：真 → 真 = 真</span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>H ↔ ¬L：真 ↔ 真 = 真</span></p></li></ul></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>但S4 → L：真 → 假 = 假</span><br><span>因此，KB ⊭ S4 → L</span></p></li></ul><h4><span>是否蕴含：如果肿瘤不是4期，则它预后良好？</span></h4><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>蕴含。从KB可得：</span></p><ul><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>¬S4 → (¬M ∧ B)  [来自公理2]</span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>B → G  [来自公理3]</span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>因此¬S4 → G</span><br><span>在所有满足KB的模型中，¬S4 → G都为真，所以KB ⊨ ¬S4 → G</span></p></li></ul><h3><span>问题1.3</span></h3><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>一阶逻辑知识库𝒦：</span></p><ol start="1"><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>∀x(VSD(x) → CHD(x))</span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>∀x(AS(x) → CHD(x))</span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>∀x(VSD(x) → ∃y(Septum(y) ∧ affects(x,y)))</span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>∀x(Septum(x) → Tissue(x) ∧ ∃y(LHeart(y) ∧ partOf(x,y)) ∧ ∃z(RHeart(z) ∧ partOf(x,z)))</span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>∀x(Heart(x) → Organ(x))</span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>∃x(GATA4(x) ∧ Gene(x) ∧ ∃y(VSD(y) ∧ relatedTo(x,y)))</span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>∀x(AS(x) → ∃y(Heart(y) ∧ suffersCondition(y,x) ∧ ∃z(TrieValve(z) ∧ partOf(z,y) ∧ hasDisPart(y,z))))</span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>∀x(Heart(x) ∧ ∃y(TrieValve(y) ∧ partOf(y,x) ∧ hasDisPart(x,y)) → ∃z(CHD(z) ∧ suffersCondition(x,z)))</span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>∀x∀y∀z(partOf(x,y) ∧ partOf(y,z) ∧ Organ(z) → partOf(x,z))</span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>∀x(CHD(x) → ∀y(affects(x,y) → ∃z(Heart(z) ∧ partOf(y,z))))</span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>∃x(Murmur(x) ∧ ∃y(CHD(y) ∧ symptomOf(x,y)))</span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>∃x(Murmur(x) ∧ ¬∃y(CHD(y) ∧ symptomOf(x,y)))</span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>∀x(Auscultation(x) → MedProc(x) ∧ ¬SurProc(x))</span></p></li></ol><h3><span>问题1.4</span></h3><h4><span>家庭关系的Datalog规则</span></h4><ul><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>Father(x,y) ← Parent(x,y), Male(x)</span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>Mother(x,y) ← Parent(x,y), Female(x)</span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>Son(x,y) ← Parent(y,x), Male(x)</span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>Daughter(x,y) ← Parent(y,x), Female(x)</span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>Sibling(x,y) ← Parent(z,x), Parent(z,y), x ≠ y</span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>Brother(x,y) ← Sibling(x,y), Male(x)</span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>Sister(x,y) ← Sibling(x,y), Female(x)</span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>Grandparent(x,y) ← Parent(x,z), Parent(z,y)</span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>Uncle(x,y) ← Parent(z,y), Brother(x,z)</span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>Cousin(x,y) ← Parent(a,x), Parent(b,y), Sibling(a,b)</span></p></li></ul><h4><span>Datalog的表达性限制</span></h4><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>Datalog不能直接表达：</span></p><ul><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>否定条件（如"x没有孩子"）</span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>头部的存在量词</span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>复杂的关系如"继兄弟姐妹"或"同父异母的兄弟姐妹"</span></p></li></ul><h3><span>问题1.5</span></h3><h4><span>1. 使用反向链接证明John是Peter的祖父母</span></h4><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>目标：GrandParent(john, peter)</span></p><ul><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>匹配规则：GrandParent(x,z) ← Parent(x,y), Parent(y,z)</span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>统一：x = john, z = peter</span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>子目标1：Parent(john,y)</span></p><ul><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>从Father(john, mary)和规则Father(x,y) → Parent(x,y)得Parent(john, mary)，y = mary</span></p></li></ul></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>子目标2：Parent(mary,peter)</span></p><ul><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>从Mother(mary, peter)和规则Mother(x,y) → Parent(x,y)得Parent(mary, peter)</span></p></li></ul></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>因此，GrandParent(john, peter)得证</span></p></li></ul><h4><span>2. 使用前向链接证明Mary和David是兄弟姐妹</span></h4><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>前向链接过程：</span></p><ul><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>初始事实：Father(john, mary), Mother(mary, peter), Father(john, david)</span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>应用Father(x,y) → Parent(x,y)：</span></p><ul><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>Parent(john, mary) [来自Father(john, mary)]</span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>Parent(john, david) [来自Father(john, david)]</span></p></li></ul></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>应用Mother(x,y) → Parent(x,y)：</span></p><ul><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>Parent(mary, peter) [来自Mother(mary, peter)]</span></p></li></ul></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>应用Parent(x,y) ∧ Parent(x,z) → Sibling(y,z)：</span></p><ul><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>取x = john, y = mary, z = david</span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>有Parent(john, mary)和Parent(john, david)</span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>因此推导出Sibling(mary, david)</span></p></li></ul></li></ul><h3><span>问题1.6</span></h3><h4><span>D-ENTAILMENT问题算法</span></h4><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><strong><span>输入</span></strong><span>：有限的析取规则集合ℛ，有限的基事实集合ℱ，无函数符号的基原子α</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><strong><span>输出</span></strong><span>：如果ℛ ∪ ℱ的每个模型都是α的模型，则返回真；否则返回假</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><strong><span>算法步骤</span></strong><span>：</span></p><ol start="1"><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>令C为ℱ和ℛ中出现的所有常量集合。如果C为空，引入一个虚拟常量</span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>将ℛ中所有规则通过用C中常量替换变量进行实例化，得到基规则集合G</span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>令S = G ∪ ℱ ∪ {¬α}</span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>检查S是否不可满足：</span></p><ul><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>如果S不可满足，返回真（ℛ ∪ ℱ ⊨ α）</span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>如果S可满足，返回假（ℛ ∪ ℱ ⊭ α）</span></p></li></ul></li></ol><h4><span>算法正确性说明</span></h4><ul><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>由于规则无函数符号，赫尔布朗宇宙有限，实例化后的G是有限的</span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>ℛ ∪ ℱ ⊨ α 当且仅当 ℛ ∪ ℱ ∪ {¬α} 不可满足</span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>命题逻辑的不可满足性问题是可判定的</span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>该算法虽然可能效率不高，但能正确解决D-ENTAILMENT问题</span></p></li></ul>

---

### 用户

12. Every medical procedure is either surgical or non-surgical, and no medical procedure can be
 surgical and non-surgical at the same time.把这句表述用fol写

---

### DeepSeek AI

<p>思考：</p><blockquote><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>首先，用户要求将第12条陈述用一阶逻辑（FOL）表示。陈述是：“Every medical procedure is either surgical or non-surgical, and no medical procedure can be surgical and non-surgical at the same time.”</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>我需要使用提供的谓词。从问题中，我知道有以下谓词：</span></p><ul><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>MedProc(x)：x 是一个医疗过程</span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>SurProc(x)：x 是一个外科过程</span></p></li></ul><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>但陈述中提到了“surgical”和“non-surgical”。我认为“surgical”对应于SurProc(x)，但“non-surgical”没有直接的谓词。从问题1.3中，有Auscultation(x)，</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>它被定义为一种非外科医疗过程。所以，我可能需要定义一个谓词来表示非外科过程，或者直接使用否定。</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>回顾问题1.3的规范，我看到了Auscultation(x)，但并没有明确的“NonSurgical”谓词。在公理13中，有：∀x (Auscultation(x) → MedProc(x) ∧ ¬SurProc(x))，但这只针对听诊。</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>对于一般性的“non-surgical”，我应该使用¬SurProc(x)来表示非外科过程。</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>所以，陈述12说：每个医疗过程要么是外科的，要么是非外科的，并且不能同时是外科和非外科。</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>这可以分解为两个部分：</span></p><ol start="1"><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>每个医疗过程是外科的或非外科的。</span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>没有医疗过程同时是外科和非外科的。</span></p></li></ol><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>在FOL中，这可以写为：</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>∀x (MedProc(x) → (SurProc(x) ∨ ¬SurProc(x)))</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>但¬SurProc(x)就是非外科的，所以第一部分实际上是重言式，因为SurProc(x) ∨ ¬SurProc(x)总是真。所以，第一部分不需要明确写出，因为它是逻辑真。</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>但陈述的第二部分说“不能同时是外科和非外科的”，这相当于说SurProc(x)和¬SurProc(x)不能同时真，这也是逻辑真。所以，整个陈述在逻辑上是冗余的，因为它只是表达了排中律和非矛盾律。</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>然而，在知识库中，我们通常不会写出逻辑真值，但既然问题要求形式化，我可能需要写出它，以反映原始陈述。</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>但再看问题1.3，在给出的知识库中，我没有看到针对陈述12的公理。可能因为它被认为是隐含的。</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>但用户明确要求写出这个陈述，所以我应该写出它。</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>在FOL中，我们可以写：</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>∀x (MedProc(x) → (SurProc(x) ∨ ¬SurProc(x)))</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>但这总是真，所以没有信息量。</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>更精确地，陈述可能意在定义医疗过程的分类：每个医疗过程要么是外科的，要么是非外科的，但这里“非外科的”可能不是一个独立的谓词，而是通过SurProc的否定来表示。</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>所以，为了捕捉“要么外科要么非外科”，我们不需要额外的公理，因为它是逻辑真。</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>但第二部分“不能同时是外科和非外科的”也是逻辑真。</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>所以，实际上，这个陈述在FOL中不需要任何公理，因为它已经由逻辑保证。</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>然而，在知识库中，我们可能想确保SurProc是互斥的，但既然只有一个谓词，它自动是互斥的。</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>或许我误解了。可能“surgical”和“non-surgical”都是谓词？但问题中只提供了SurProc，没有NonSurgical谓词。</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>在问题1.3的谓词列表中，有SurProc，但没有NonSurgical。所以，我认为“non-surgical”就是用¬SurProc来表示。</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>因此，陈述12在FOL中不需要任何额外的公理。</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>但用户要求写出它，所以我应该写出一个公理，即使它是冗余。</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>或许在上下文中，我们需要定义医疗过程的类型。</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>另一个想法：可能“non-surgical”不是一个正式的谓词，但我们需要表达每个医疗过程要么是SurProc要么不是。</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>但如前所述，这是逻辑真。</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>或许陈述12是为了强调分类的完备性和互斥性。</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>在FOL中，我们可以写：</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>∀x (MedProc(x) → (SurProc(x) ∨ ¬SurProc(x)))</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>但这总是真。</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>为了表达互斥性，我们已经有那个不能同时真，这也是逻辑真。</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>所以，我认为在知识库中，这个陈述不需要显式公理。</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>但在问题1.3的示例答案中，我没有包含它，所以对于用户的问题，我可以说不需要公理。</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>但用户直接问了这个陈述，所以我应该提供FOL表示。</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>让我看用户的消息："12. Every medical procedure is either surgical or non-surgical, and no medical procedure can be surgical and non-surgical at the same time.把这句表述用fol写"</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>所以，我需要用FOL写这个句子。</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>使用谓词 MedProc(x) 和 SurProc(x)。</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>“surgical” 就是 SurProc(x)，“non-surgical” 就是 ¬SurProc(x)。</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>所以，“every medical procedure is either surgical or non-surgical” 是 ∀x (MedProc(x) → (SurProc(x) ∨ ¬SurProc(x)))</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>但如前所述，这等价于 ∀x (MedProc(x) → True)， which is always true.</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>“no medical procedure can be surgical and non-surgical at the same time” 是 ∀x (MedProc(x) → ¬(SurProc(x) ∧ ¬SurProc(x)))</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>这等价于 ∀x (MedProc(x) → ¬False) = ∀x (MedProc(x) → True)， which is also always true.</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>所以，整个陈述在FOL中是一个重言式，因此不需要显式写出。</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>但或许在上下文中，我们有一个谓词用于“non-surgical”，但问题中没有这样的谓词。</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>另一个想法：或许“non-surgical”是一个不同的谓词，比如 NonSurProc(x)，但问题中没有定义这个谓词。</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>在谓词列表中，只有 SurProc，没有 NonSurProc。 所以，我认为使用 ¬SurProc 是正确的。</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>因此，对于这个陈述，在FOL中不需要任何公理。</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>但为了满足用户的要求，我可以写出：</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>∀x (MedProc(x) → (SurProc(x) ∨ ¬SurProc(x))) ∧ ∀x (MedProc(x) → ¬(SurProc(x) ∧ ¬SurProc(x)))</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>但这冗余且总是真。</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>或许陈述12是为了说明医疗过程只能有两种类型，并且这两种类型是互斥的，但既然我们只有一个谓词 SurProc，那么非外科就是其否定，所以分类是完备且互斥的。</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>所以，我认为在知识库中，我们不需要添加任何东西。</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>对于用户的请求，我可以说这个陈述在FOL中是一个逻辑真，因此不需要显式公理。</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>但既然用户要求写出，我就写出它。</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>在问题1.3的答案中，我包含了公理13 for Auscultation, but not for general medical procedures.</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>所以，对于陈述12，我可以写：</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>∀x (MedProc(x) → SurProc(x) ∨ ¬SurProc(x))</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>但这没有意义。</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>或许我错过了什么。 让我们读一下原始问题中的陈述12: "Every medical procedure is either surgical or non-surgical, and no medical procedure can be surgical and non-surgical at the same time."</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>在知识库中，我们可能想确保每个医疗过程都被分类为外科或非外科，但既然非外科没有独立谓词，这似乎有点奇怪。</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>在公理13中，我们有 Auscultation 是非外科的，但还有其他非外科过程吗？</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>或许我们需要定义 NonSurProc 谓词，但问题中没有给出。</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>在谓词列表中，只有 SurProc，所以我认为 SurProc 是唯一的谓词用于外科过程，而非外科过程就是那些不是 SurProc 的医疗过程。</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>所以，陈述12在FOL中不需要显式表示。</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>对于用户的响应，我可以说明这一点。</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>但为了直接回答，我将提供FOL公式。</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>所以，FOL表示是：</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>∀x (MedProc(x) → (SurProc(x) ∨ ¬SurProc(x))) ∧ ∀x (MedProc(x) → ¬(SurProc(x) ∧ ¬SurProc(x)))</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>但如前所述，这等价于 True。</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>所以，一个更简洁的方式是写一个公理 that says that every medical procedure is exactly one of surgical or non-surgical, but since non-surgical is not a predicate, we can't do that without introducing a new predicate.</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>或许在上下文中，"non-surgical" 是通过其他方式隐含的。</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>我认为对于这个练习，我们不需要为陈述12添加公理。</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>在问题1.3的示例答案中，我没有包含它，所以对于用户，我可以说在知识库中不需要额外的公理。</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>但既然用户专门问了这个，我会提供FOL代码。</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>让我们定义一个新的谓词？但用户说“使用以下谓词”，所以我不应该添加新谓词。</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>所以，使用给定的谓词，唯一的方式是使用 SurProc。</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>因此，FOL for statement 12 is logically true, so no axiom is needed.</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>在响应中，我可以写：由于“外科”和“非外科”是互斥的，并且覆盖了所有医疗过程，这个陈述在逻辑上为真，因此在一阶逻辑中不需要显式公理。</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>但为了完整，我可以用FOL写出来。</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>或许陈述12是为了强调医疗过程的分类，所以在FOL中，我们可以写：</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>∀x (MedProc(x) → SurProc(x) ∨ ¬SurProc(x))</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>但这总是真。</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>我放弃了。</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>另一个想法：或许“surgical”和“non-surgical”是医疗过程的属性，但既然我们只有 SurProc，那么“non-surgical”就是 ¬SurProc，所以陈述12没有提供新信息。</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>所以，在知识库中，我们不需要为它写公理。</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>对于用户的问题，我会说这个陈述在一阶逻辑中是一个重言式，因此不需要显式表示。</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>但为了写出点东西，我会提供以下内容：</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>∀x (MedProc(x) → (SurProc(x) ∨ ¬SurProc(x))) ∧ ∀x (MedProc(x) → ¬(SurProc(x) ∧ ¬SurProc(x)))</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>但这是不必要的。</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>或许在知识库中，我们有一个公理 that defines that surgical and non-surgical are disjoint, but again, it's logical.</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>我认为我应该继续前进并提供响应。</span></p></blockquote><br/><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>根据问题1.3中提供的谓词，陈述12：“Every medical procedure is either surgical or non-surgical, and no medical procedure can be surgical and non-surgical at the same time” 可以用一阶逻辑（FOL）表示如下：</span></p><ul><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>使用谓词：MedProc(x) 表示 x 是医疗过程，SurProc(x) 表示 x 是外科过程。</span></p></li><li><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>“non-surgical” 可以通过 ¬SurProc(x) 来表示。</span></p></li></ul><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>因此，陈述12的FOL形式为：</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>∀x (MedProc(x) → (SurProc(x) ∨ ¬SurProc(x))) ∧ ∀x (MedProc(x) → ¬(SurProc(x) ∧ ¬SurProc(x)))</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>然而，这个公式在逻辑上是一个重言式（总是真），因为它反映了排中律和非矛盾律。在知识库中，通常不需要显式包含这样的重言式，因为它不会增加新的信息。但既然您要求形式化，这就是对应的FOL表示。</span></p><p class="ds-markdown-paragraph"><span>在问题1.3的知识库中，这个陈述没有显式包含，因为它是逻辑隐含的。</span></p>
